\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01277}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a0bb134560ed6083c96e98027355aee31}{01277}}     \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a0bb134560ed6083c96e98027355aee31}{getweisamcovuppmeantrans}}(np,sumWeight,nd,Point,Weight,CovMatUpper,Mean)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01278}01278 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if INTEL\_COMPILER\_ENABLED \&\& defined DLL\_ENABLED \&\& (OS\_IS\_WINDOWS || defined OS\_IS\_DARWIN)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01279}01279 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}        \textcolor{comment}{!DEC\$ ATTRIBUTES DLLEXPORT :: getWeiSamCovUppMeanTrans}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01280}01280 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01281}01281 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01282}01282         \textcolor{keywordtype}{use }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacematrix__mod}{matrix\_mod}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{only}: \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacematrix__mod_a390563b2761c2e0cca18a38562bacf1c}{getinvposdefmatsqrtdet}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01283}01283         \textcolor{keywordtype}{implicit none}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01284}01284         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}             :: np,nd,sumWeight        \textcolor{comment}{! np is the number of observations, nd is the number of parameters for each observation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01285}01285         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}             :: Weight(np)             \textcolor{comment}{! weights of the points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01286}01286 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}             :: Point(nd,np)           \textcolor{comment}{! Point is the matrix of the data, CovMatUpper contains the elements of the sample covariance matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01287}01287 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)}            :: CovMatUpper(nd,nd)     \textcolor{comment}{! Covariance matrix of the input data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01288}01288 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)}            :: Mean(nd)               \textcolor{comment}{! Mean vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01289}01289 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)                            :: sumWeightMinusOneInvReal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01290}01290 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)                            :: NormData(nd,np)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01291}01291         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}                         :: i,j,ip}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01292}01292 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01293}01293         mean = 0.\_rk}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01294}01294         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1,np}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01295}01295             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} j = 1,nd}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01296}01296                 mean(j) = mean(j) + weight(i)*point(j,i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01297}01297 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01298}01298 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01299}01299         mean = mean / real(sumweight,kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01300}01300 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01301}01301         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1,np}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01302}01302             normdata(1:nd,i) = point(1:nd,i) -\/ mean}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01303}01303 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01304}01304 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01305}01305         sumweightminusoneinvreal = 1.\_rk / real(sumweight-\/1,kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01306}01306         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} j = 1,nd}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01307}01307             \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} i = 1,j}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01308}01308                 covmatupper(i,j) = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01309}01309                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} ip = 1,np}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01310}01310                     covmatupper(i,j) = covmatupper(i,j) + weight(ip)*normdata(i,ip)*normdata(j,ip)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01311}01311 \textcolor{keywordflow}{                end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01312}01312                 covmatupper(i,j) = covmatupper(i,j) * sumweightminusoneinvreal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01313}01313 \textcolor{keywordflow}{            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01314}01314 \textcolor{keywordflow}{        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01315}01315 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01316}01316     \textcolor{keyword}{end subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a0bb134560ed6083c96e98027355aee31}{getweisamcovuppmeantrans}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01341}01341     \textcolor{comment}{! This subroutine uses a recursion equation similar to http://stats.stackexchange.com/questions/97642/how-\/to-\/combine-\/sample-\/means-\/and-\/sample-\/variances}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01345}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a5654bd399eda22aded1a4b445d968b87}{01345}}     \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a5654bd399eda22aded1a4b445d968b87}{mergemeancov}}(nd,npA,MeanVecA,CovMatA,npB,MeanVecB,CovMatB,MeanVecAB,CovMatAB)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01346}01346 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if INTEL\_COMPILER\_ENABLED \&\& defined DLL\_ENABLED \&\& (OS\_IS\_WINDOWS || defined OS\_IS\_DARWIN)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01347}01347 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}        \textcolor{comment}{!DEC\$ ATTRIBUTES DLLEXPORT :: mergeMeanCov}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01348}01348 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01349}01349 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}        \textcolor{keywordtype}{implicit none}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01350}01350         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}       :: nd}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01351}01351         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}       :: npA,npB}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01352}01352 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}       :: MeanVecA(nd),CovMatA(nd,nd)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01353}01353 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(in)}       :: MeanVecB(nd),CovMatB(nd,nd)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01354}01354 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{intent(out)}      :: MeanVecAB(nd),CovMatAB(nd,nd)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01355}01355 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)   , \textcolor{keywordtype}{dimension(nd,1)}  :: MeanMatA,MeanMatB,MeanMat}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01356}01356 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)                      :: DistanceSq(nd,nd)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01357}01357 \textcolor{keywordtype}{        real}(RK)                      :: npABinverse}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01358}01358         \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer(IK)}                   :: npAB}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01359}01359 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01360}01360         npab = npa + npb}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01361}01361         npabinverse = 1.\_rk / real(npab, kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01362}01362         meanmata(1:nd,1) = meanveca}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01363}01363         meanmatb(1:nd,1) = meanvecb}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01364}01364 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01365}01365         \textcolor{comment}{! Compute the new Mean}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01366}01366 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01367}01367         meanvecab = ( npa * meanveca + npb * meanvecb ) * npabinverse}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01368}01368         meanmat(1:nd,1) = meanvecab}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01369}01369 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01370}01370         \textcolor{comment}{! Compute the new Covariance matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01371}01371 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01372}01372         distancesq = matmul( (meanmata-\/meanmatb), transpose((meanmata-\/meanmatb)) ) * npa * npb * npabinverse}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01373}01373         covmatab = ( (npa-\/1) * covmata + (npb-\/1) * covmatb + distancesq ) / real(npab-\/1, kind=rk)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01374}01374 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01375}01375     \textcolor{keyword}{end subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a5654bd399eda22aded1a4b445d968b87}{mergemeancov}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01377}01377 \textcolor{comment}{!\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01379}01379 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)brief}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01380}01380 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> Given two input sample means and covariance matrices, return the combination of them as a single mean and covariance matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01381}01381 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01382}01382 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       nd              :   The number of dimensions of the input sample.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01383}01383 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       npA             :   The number of points in sample `A`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01384}01384 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       MeanVecA        :   The mean vector of sample `A`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01385}01385 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       CovMatUpperA    :   The covariance matrix of sample `A`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01386}01386 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       npB             :   The number of points in sample `B`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01387}01387 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       MeanVecB        :   The mean vector of sample `B`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01388}01388 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]       CovMatUpperB    :   The covariance matrix of sample `B`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01389}01389 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[out]      MeanVecAB       :   The output mean vector of the combined sample.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01390}01390 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[out]      CovMatUpperAB   :   The output covariance matrix of the combined sample.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01391}01391 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01392}01392 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)todo}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01393}01393 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> The efficiency of this algorithm might still be improved by converting the upper triangle covariance matrix to a packed vector.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01394}01394 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01395}01395 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)remark}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01396}01396 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> This subroutine is the same as [mergeMeanCov](@ref mergeMeanCov), with the **important difference** that only the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01397}01397 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> upper triangles and diagonals of the input covariance matrices need to be given by the user: `CovMatUpperA`, `CovMatUpperB`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01398}01398 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> This alternative implementation is 6-\/7 times faster, with all compiler optimization flags on.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01399}01399 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01400}01400 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)author}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01401}01401 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> Amir Shahmoradi, Nov 24, 2020, 4:19 AM, Dallas, TX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01402}01402 \textcolor{comment}{!    subroutine mergeMeanCovUpperSlow(nd,npA,MeanVecA,CovMatUpperA,npB,MeanVecB,CovMatUpperB,MeanVecAB,CovMatUpperAB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01403}01403 \textcolor{comment}{!\#if INTEL\_COMPILER\_ENABLED \&\& defined DLL\_ENABLED \&\& (OS\_IS\_WINDOWS || defined OS\_IS\_DARWIN)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01404}01404 \textcolor{comment}{!        !DEC\$ ATTRIBUTES DLLEXPORT :: mergeMeanCovUpperSlow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01405}01405 \textcolor{comment}{!\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01406}01406 \textcolor{comment}{!        implicit none}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01407}01407 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK), intent(in)             :: nd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01408}01408 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK), intent(in)             :: npA,npB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01409}01409 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)   , intent(in)             :: MeanVecA(nd),CovMatUpperA(nd,nd)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01410}01410 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)   , intent(in)             :: MeanVecB(nd),CovMatUpperB(nd,nd)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01411}01411 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)   , intent(out)            :: MeanVecAB(nd),CovMatUpperAB(nd,nd)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01412}01412 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)                            :: npABinverse, npAnpB2npAB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01413}01413 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)                            :: npA2npAB, npB2npAB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01414}01414 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)                            :: MeanVecDiffAB(nd)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01415}01415 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK)                         :: npAB, i, j}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01416}01416 \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01417}01417 \textcolor{comment}{!        npAB = npA + npB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01418}01418 \textcolor{comment}{!        npABinverse = 1.\_RK / real(npAB, kind=RK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01419}01419 \textcolor{comment}{!        npAnpB2npAB = npA * npB * npABinverse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01420}01420 \textcolor{comment}{!        npA2npAB = npA * npABinverse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01421}01421 \textcolor{comment}{!        npB2npAB = npB * npABinverse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01422}01422 \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01423}01423 \textcolor{comment}{!        ! Compute the new Mean and Covariance matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01424}01424 \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01425}01425 \textcolor{comment}{!        do j = 1, nd}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01426}01426 \textcolor{comment}{!            MeanVecDiffAB(j) = MeanVecA(j) -\/ MeanVecB(j)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01427}01427 \textcolor{comment}{!            !MeanVecAB(j) = ( npA * MeanVecA(j) + npB * MeanVecB(j) ) * npABinverse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01428}01428 \textcolor{comment}{!            MeanVecAB(j) = npA2npAB * MeanVecA(j) + npB2npAB * MeanVecB(j)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01429}01429 \textcolor{comment}{!            do i = 1, j}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01430}01430 \textcolor{comment}{!                CovMatUpperAB(i,j) = ( (npA-\/1) * CovMatUpperA(i,j) + (npB-\/1) * CovMatUpperB(i,j) + MeanVecDiffAB(i) * MeanVecDiffAB(j) * npAnpB2npAB ) / real(npAB-\/1, kind=RK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01431}01431 \textcolor{comment}{!            end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01432}01432 \textcolor{comment}{!        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01433}01433 \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01434}01434 \textcolor{comment}{!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01435}01435 \textcolor{comment}{!    end subroutine mergeMeanCovUpperSlow}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01685}01685     \textcolor{comment}{! Given the mean vector MeanVec and the covariance matrix CovMat, this subroutine generates a random vector x (of length nd>=2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01686}01686     \textcolor{comment}{! from an nd-\/dimensional multivariate normal distribution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01687}01687     \textcolor{comment}{! First a vector of nd standard normal random deviates is generated,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01688}01688     \textcolor{comment}{! then this vector is multiplied by the Cholesky decomposition of the covariance matrix,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01689}01689     \textcolor{comment}{! then the vector MeanVec is added to the resulting vector, and is stored in the output vector x.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01690}01690     \textcolor{comment}{! ATTENTION: Only the upper half of the covariance matrix (plus the diagonal terms) need to be given in the input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01691}01691     \textcolor{comment}{! in the ouput, the upper half and diagonal part will still be the covariance matrix, while the lower half will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01692}01692     \textcolor{comment}{! the Cholesky decomposition elements (excluding its diagonal terms that are provided only in the vector Diagonal).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01693}01693     \textcolor{comment}{! USES choldc.f90, getRandGaus.f90}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l01695}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a909b74c0f3765b348333424084a4aa4c}{01695}}     \textcolor{keyword}{subroutine }\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacestatistics__mod_a909b74c0f3765b348333424084a4aa4c}{getmvndev}}(nd,MeanVec,CovMat,X)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02800}02800 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)brief}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02801}02801 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> Return the Geometric distribution PDF values for a range of trials, starting at index `1`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02802}02802 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> If the probability of success on each trial is `successProb`, then the probability that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02803}02803 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> the `k`th trial (out of `k` trials) is the first success is `GeoLogPDF(k)`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02804}02804 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02805}02805 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   successProb     :   The probability of success.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02806}02806 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   logPdfPrecision :   The precision value below which the PDF is practically considered to be zero (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02807}02807 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   minSeqLen       :   The minimum length of the range of `k` values for which the PDF will be computed (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02808}02808 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)param[in]   seqLen          :   The length of the range of `k` values for which the PDF will be computed (**optional**).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02809}02809 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>                                  If provided, it will overwrite the the output sequence length as inferred from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02810}02810 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>                                  the combination of `minSeqLen` and `logPdfPrecision`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02811}02811 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02812}02812 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02813}02813 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> `GeoLogPDF`  :   An allocatable representing the geometric PDF over a range of `k` values, whose length is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02814}02814 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>                  `seqLen`, or if not provided, is determined from the values of `logPdfPrecision` and `minSeqLen`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02815}02815 \textcolor{comment}{!    !>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02816}02816 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> \(\backslash\)author}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02817}02817 \textcolor{comment}{!    !> Amir Shahmoradi, Monday March 6, 2017, 3:22 pm, ICES, The University of Texas at Austin.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02818}02818 \textcolor{comment}{!    function getGeoLogPDF\_old(successProb,logPdfPrecision,minSeqLen,seqLen) result(GeoLogPDF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02819}02819 \textcolor{comment}{!\#if INTEL\_COMPILER\_ENABLED \&\& defined DLL\_ENABLED \&\& (OS\_IS\_WINDOWS || defined OS\_IS\_DARWIN)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02824}02824 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)    , intent(in)            :: successProb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02825}02825 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)    , intent(in), optional  :: logPdfPrecision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02826}02826 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK) , intent(in), optional  :: minSeqLen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02827}02827 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK) , intent(in), optional  :: seqLen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02828}02828 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)    , allocatable           :: GeoLogPDF(:)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02829}02829 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)    , parameter             :: LOG\_PDF\_PRECISION = log(0.001\_RK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02830}02830 \textcolor{comment}{!        real(RK)                            :: logProbFailure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02831}02831 \textcolor{comment}{!        integer(IK)                         :: lenGeoLogPDF, i}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02832}02832 \textcolor{comment}{!        logProbFailure = log(1.\_RK -\/ successProb)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02833}02833 \textcolor{comment}{!        if (present(seqLen)) then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02834}02834 \textcolor{comment}{!            lenGeoLogPDF = seqLen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02835}02835 \textcolor{comment}{!        else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02836}02836 \textcolor{comment}{!            if (present(logPdfPrecision)) then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02837}02837 \textcolor{comment}{!                lenGeoLogPDF = ceiling(  logPdfPrecision / logProbFailure)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02838}02838 \textcolor{comment}{!            else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02839}02839 \textcolor{comment}{!                lenGeoLogPDF = ceiling(LOG\_PDF\_PRECISION / logProbFailure)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02840}02840 \textcolor{comment}{!            end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02841}02841 \textcolor{comment}{!            if (present(minSeqLen)) lenGeoLogPDF = max(minSeqLen,lenGeoLogPDF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02842}02842 \textcolor{comment}{!        end if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02843}02843 \textcolor{comment}{!        allocate(GeoLogPDF(lenGeoLogPDF))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02844}02844 \textcolor{comment}{!        GeoLogPDF(1) = log(successProb)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02845}02845 \textcolor{comment}{!        do i = 2, lenGeoLogPDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02846}02846 \textcolor{comment}{!            GeoLogPDF(i) = GeoLogPDF(i-\/1) + logProbFailure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02847}02847 \textcolor{comment}{!        end do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{Statistics__mod_8f90_source_l02848}02848 \textcolor{comment}{!    end function getGeoLogPDF\_old}}
